<script type="text/javascript">

function Check() {
	var value = document.getElementById('designer1_ctl04_Login1_pcLogin_edit_Phone1').value;
	//if (value.substr(0, 1) =="+" && value.length > 10)
}
setInterval('Check()',1000);

function numbersonly(e, decimal) {
		var key;
		var keychar;

		if (window.event) {
		   key = window.event.keyCode;
		}
		else if (e) {
		   key = e.which;
		}
		else {
		   return true;
		}
		keychar = String.fromCharCode(key);

		if ((key==null) || (key==0) || (key==8) ||  (key==9) || (key==13) || (key==27) ) {
		   return true;
		}
		else if ((("+0123456789").indexOf(keychar) > -1)) {
		   return true;
		}
		else if (decimal && (keychar == ".")) {
		  return true;
		}
		else
		   return false;
}

function RemoveUsernameText(control) {
	if (control.value=='Vartotojo vardas (el. paštas)')
	    control.value = '';
}

function AddUsernameText(control) {
	if (control.value=='')
	    control.value = 'Vartotojo vardas (el. paštas)';
}

function RemovePasswordText(control) {
	if (control.value=='Slaptažodis')
	    control.value = '';
}

function AddPasswordText(control) {
	if (control.value=='')
	    control.value = 'Slaptažodis';
}

</script>

function CheckLeft() {
	var value = document.getElementById('designer1_ctl08_LoginSwitch1_ctl00_pcLogin_edit_Phone1').value;
	//if (value.substr(0, 1) =="+" && value.length > 10)
    if (value.length === 7)

function numbersonly(e, decimal) {
		var key;
		var keychar;

		if (window.event) {
		   key = window.event.keyCode;
		}
		else if (e) {
		   key = e.which;
		}
		else {
		   return true;
		}
		keychar = String.fromCharCode(key);

		if ((key==null) || (key==0) || (key==8) ||  (key==9) || (key==13) || (key==27) ) {
		   return true;
		}
		else if ((("+0123456789").indexOf(keychar) > -1)) {
		   return true;
		}
		else if (decimal && (keychar == ".")) {
		  return true;
		}
		else
		   return false;
}

function RemoveUsernameTextLeft(control) {
	if (control.value=='Vartotojo vardas (el. paštas)')
	    control.value = '';
}

function AddUsernameTextLeft(control) {
	if (control.value=='')
	    control.value = 'Vartotojo vardas (el. paštas)';
}

function RemovePasswordTextLeft(control) {
	if (control.value=='Slaptažodis')
	    control.value = '';
}

function AddPasswordTextLeft(control) {
	if (control.value=='')
	    control.value = 'Slaptažodis';
}

    document.body.scrollTop = 0; // For Safari
    document.documentElement.scrollTop = 0; // For Chrome, Firefox, IE and Opera
    popupForgotLeft.Show();
}

    popupBadLogin.Show();

}

<script type="text/javascript">
function DoCompare() {
	var check = ValidateCheckBox('Pažymėkite bent vieną prekę!');
	if (check)
	{

		var params = '';
		var n = 0;
		var ml = document.forms[0];
		var len = ml.elements.length;
		for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) {
		    var e = ml.elements[i];
			if (e.name.indexOf( name )>=0 && e.checked == true) {
				params += ',' + e.value;
				n++;
				if (n > 5) {
					alert('Per daug pažymėjote įrašų!');
					return;
				}
			}
		}
		OnComparePrint('LT', 'EUR', params);
	}
}



function evaluateObjectResult( source ) {
	var destination = 'designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_InputQuantity';
	var destinationId = document.getElementById( destination );

	destinationId.value = source.value;
}

function OnToCartSells( id, quantity )
{
	var quantityId = document.getElementById( quantity );
	url = window.document.URL.replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|");
	SetCookie("url", url);

	location.href = 'default.aspx?Page=ToCart&CartType=CatalogStore&ID=' + id + '&Q=' + quantityId.value + '&CatID=&SearchPage=CatalogStore&criteria=samsung s8';
}

function OnToCartUnload( id, quantity, IsCentral )
{
	var quantityId = document.getElementById( quantity );
	url = window.document.URL.replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|");
	SetCookie("url", url);

	location.href = 'default.aspx?Page=ToCart&CartType=CatalogUnload&ID=' + id + '&Q=' + quantityId.value + '&CatID=&SearchPage=CatalogStore&criteria=samsung s8&IsCentral=' + IsCentral + '';
}

function OnToCartOrder( id, quantity )
{
	var quantityId = document.getElementById( quantity );
	url = window.document.URL.replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|").replace("=", "|");
	SetCookie("url", url);

	location.href = 'default.aspx?Page=ToCart&CartType=CatalogOrders&ID=' + id + '&Q=' + quantityId.value + '&CatID=&SearchPage=CatalogStore&criteria=samsung s8';
}

    <script type="text/javascript">
        function numbersonly(e, decimal) {
		        var key;
		        var keychar;

		        if (window.event) {
		           key = window.event.keyCode;
		        }
		        else if (e) {
		           key = e.which;
		        }
		        else {
		           return true;
		        }
		        keychar = String.fromCharCode(key);

		        if ((key==null) || (key==0) || (key==8) ||  (key==9) || (key==13) || (key==27) ) {
		           return true;
		        }
		        else if ((("0123456789").indexOf(keychar) > -1)) {
		           return true;
		        }
		        else if (decimal && (keychar === "." || keychar === ",")) {
		          return true;
		        }
		        else
		           return false;
        }
    </script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
	    maxPrice = 945; // value įrašoma maksimali reikšmė
	    minPrice = 2; // value įrašoma minimali reikšmė

	    function DoPriceFilterPostback(param) {
	        __doPostBack('designer1$ctl11$ctl00$MainCatalogSquare1$dynamicFilter$button_price_slider', param);
	    }

	    timerSlider = null;
        function GetPriceSlider(minLimit, maxLimit, minPrice, maxPrice) {
            var xPriceSlider = new Control.Slider([$('price-filter-min'), $('price-filter-max')], 'price-filter', {
                range: $R(minLimit, maxLimit),
                sliderValue: [minPrice, maxPrice], // value įrašoma minimali irmaksimali reikšmė
                values: $R(minLimit, maxLimit),
                restricted: true,
                onChange: function(val) {
				    $('price-filter-max-display').innerHTML = val[1];
				    $('price-filter-min-display').innerHTML = val[0];
				    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').value = val[1];
				    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').value = val[0];
                    DoPriceFilterPostback('');
                },
                onSlide: function(val) {
                    $('price-filter-max-display').innerHTML = val[1];
                    $('price-filter-min-display').innerHTML = val[0];
                    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').value = val[1];
                    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').value = val[0];
                }
            });

            return xPriceSlider;
        };
	    var priceSlider = GetPriceSlider(2, 945, 2, 945);

	    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').onchange = function() {
	        var max_price = parseFloat($('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').value.replace(',','.'),10);
	        var min_price= parseFloat($('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').value.replace(',','.'),10);
	        if (isNaN(min_price)) {
	            min_price = minPrice;
	        }
	        if (isNaN(max_price)) {
	            max_price = maxPrice;
	        }
	        if( max_price > maxPrice) {
	            max_price = maxPrice;
	        }
	        if( max_price < min_price) {
	            max_price = min_price;
	        }
	        priceSlider.setValue(max_price, 1);
	        $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').value = max_price;//.toFixed(2);
	        DoPriceFilterPostback('');
	    };
	    $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').onchange = function () {
	        var max_price = parseFloat($('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_max_text').value.replace(',','.'),10);
	        var min_price= parseFloat($('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').value.replace(',','.'),10);
	        if (isNaN(min_price)) {
	            min_price = minPrice;
	        }
	        if (isNaN(max_price)) {
	            max_price = maxPrice;
	        }
	        if( min_price > max_price) {
	            min_price = max_price;
	        }
	        if( min_price < minPrice) {
	            min_price = minPrice;
	        }
	        priceSlider.setValue(min_price, 0);
	        $('designer1_ctl11_ctl00_MainCatalogSquare1_dynamicFilter_PriceFilter_price_filter_min_text').value = min_price;//.toFixed(2);
	        DoPriceFilterPostback('');
	    };
